the following steps (in order):\n27: // - Construct: Create the initial plugin structs based on the plugin(s) found in the Discovery stage.\n28: // - Decorate: Decorate the plugins with additional metadata.\n29: //\n30: // The Construct step is implemented by the ConstructFunc type.\n31: //\n32: // The Decorate step is implemented by the DecorateFunc type.\n33: type Bootstrap struct {\n34: DefaultDecorateFuncs(cfg)\n52: \t}\n53: \n54: \treturn &Bootstrap{\n55: \t\tconstructStep: opts.ConstructFunc,\n56: \t\tdecorateSteps: opts.DecorateFuncs,\n57: \t\tlog:           log.New(\"plugins.bootstrap\"),\n58: \t}\n59: }\n60: \n61: // Bootstrap will execute the Construct and Decorate steps of the Bootstrap stage.\n62: func (b *Bootstrap) Bootstrap(ctx context.Context, src plugins.PluginSource, found *plugins.FoundBundle) ([]*plugins.Plugin, error) {\n63: \tps, err := b.constructStep(ctx, src, found)\n64: \tif err != nil {\n65: \t\treturn nil, err\n66: \t}\n67: \n68: \tif len(b.decorateSteps) == 0 {\n69: \t\treturn ps, nil\n70: \t}\n71: \n72: \tbootstrappedPlugins := make([]*plugins.Plugin, 0, len(ps))\n73: \tfor _, p := range ps {\n74: \t\tvar ip *plugins.Plugin\n75: \t\tfor _, decorate := range b.decorateSteps {\n76: \t\t\tip, err = decorate(ctx, p)\n77: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n78: \t\t\t\tb.log.Error(\"Could not decorate plugin\", \"pluginId\", p.ID, \"error\", err)\n79: \t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n80: \t\t\t}\n81: \t\t}\n82: \t\tbootstrappedPlugins = append(bootstrappedPlugins, ip)\n83: \t}\n84: \n85: \treturn signature verification system is implemented across multiple components in the plugin manager and pluginsintegration packages. The system handles three main aspects: plugin manifest signing, signature validation on load, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n## Plugin Manifest Signing\\n\\nThe core signature calculation happens in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go` through the `Signature` struct which implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface. The `Calculate()` method performs the following:\\n\\n1. **Manifest Reading**: `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()` opens and reads the `MANIFEST.txt` file from the plugin's filesystem. If not found, it returns `ErrSignatureTypeUnsigned`.\\n\\n2. **Manifest Parsing and Validation**: `readPluginManifest()` decodes the PGP-signed manifest using `clearsign.Decode()` and parses the JSON payload into a `PluginManifest` struct.\\n\\n3. **Manifest Validation**: `validateManifest()` ensures all required fields are present:\\n   - Basic fields: plugin, version, keyId, time, files\\n   - V2-specific fields: signedByOrg, signedByOrgName, signatureType\\n   - Calls `Verify()` to validate the PGP signature\\n\\n4. **Signature Verification**: `Verify()` retrieves the public key via `KeyRetriever.GetPublicKey()` and validates the PGP signature using `openpgp.CheckDetachedSignature()`.\\n\\n5. **File Hash Verification**: `verifyHash()` verifies each file's SHA256 hash matches the manifest's recorded hash. It detects modified plugins by comparing hashes of actual files against manifest entries.\\n\\n6. **Signature Status Determination**: The `Calculate()` method returns:\\n   - `SignatureStatusValid` for properly signed plugins with matching hashes\\n   - `SignatureStatusInvalid` for v1 manifests or invalid signatures\\n   - `SignatureStatusModified` for valid signatures with file hash mismatches\\n   - `SignatureStatusUnsigned` for plugins without MANIFEST.txt\\n\\n## Key Retrieval System\\n\\nPlugin manifest verification requires public keys. The system supports two modes:\\n\\n**Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): The default `KeyRetriever` contains a hard-coded Grafana-signed public key with ID `7e4d0c6a708866e7`. The `GetPublicKey()` method returns this key for Grafana-signed plugins.\\n\\n**Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): When enabled via configuration, the `KeyRetriever` downloads public keys from the Grafana.com API endpoint `/plugins/ci/keys`. It caches keys in a key store with a 10-day sync interval. The `downloadKeys()` method retrieves and caches `ManifestKeys` records containing keyId and public key content. The `GetPublicKey()` method looks up keys from the cache, falling back to the default key if not found.\\n\\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go` `Service` acts as a selector, delegating to dynamic keys if enabled, otherwise using static keys.\\n\\n## Signature Validation on Load\\n\\nDuring the plugin loading pipeline, signature validation occurs in two stages:\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): The `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` method calls `signatureCalculator.Calculate()` to compute the signature status for each plugin. This populates the plugin's `Signature`, `SignatureType`, and `SignatureOrg` fields.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` and `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): The `Validation.ValidateSignature()` method is called for each bootstrapped plugin. It:\\n\\n1. Returns nil (success) if signature is valid or plugin is core\\n2. For unsigned plugins: calls `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin()` to check the allowlist\\n3. Returns error for invalid or modified signatures\\n4. Handles inherited signatures for nested child plugins\\n\\nThe validation pipeline is orchestrated in `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/validation.go` through the `Validate()` method, which runs all configured validation steps including `SignatureValidationStep()`.\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` through the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct. The `CanLoadPlugin()` method enforces the allowlist by:\\n\\n1. Allowing all plugins if signature status is not unsigned (already signed/valid)\\n2. Allowing all unsigned plugins in development mode (when `DevMode` is true)\\n3. Checking the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` list from configuration: if the plugin ID matches an entry in this list, it returns true\\n4. Returning false (rejecting the plugin) otherwise\\n\\nThe configuration is read in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` from the INI file key `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` and stored in `pkg/setting/setting.go` as part of the `Cfg` struct's `PluginsAllowUnsigned` field. signature verification system is implemented across multiple components in the plugin manager and pluginsintegration packages. The system handles three main aspects: plugin manifest signing, signature validation on load, and unsigned plugin allowlist enforcement.\\n\\n## Plugin Manifest Signing\\n\\nThe core signature calculation happens in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go` through the `Signature` struct which implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface. The `Calculate()` method performs the following:\\n\\n1. **Manifest Reading**: `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()` opens and reads the `MANIFEST.txt` file from the plugin's filesystem. If not found, it returns `ErrSignatureTypeUnsigned`.\\n\\n2. **Manifest Parsing and Validation**: `readPluginManifest()` decodes the PGP-signed manifest using `clearsign.Decode()` and parses the JSON payload into a `PluginManifest` struct.\\n\\n3. **Manifest Validation**: `validateManifest()` ensures all required fields are present:\\n   - Basic fields: plugin, version, keyId, time, files\\n   - V2-specific fields: signedByOrg, signedByOrgName, signatureType\\n   - Calls `Verify()` to validate the PGP signature\\n\\n4. **Signature Verification**: `Verify()` retrieves the public key via `KeyRetriever.GetPublicKey()` and validates the PGP signature using `openpgp.CheckDetachedSignature()`.\\n\\n5. **File Hash Verification**: `verifyHash()` verifies each file's SHA256 hash matches the manifest's recorded hash. It detects modified plugins by comparing hashes of actual files against manifest entries.\\n\\n6. **Signature Status Determination**: The `Calculate()` method returns:\\n   - `SignatureStatusValid` for properly signed plugins with matching hashes\\n   - `SignatureStatusInvalid` for v1 manifests or invalid signatures\\n   - `SignatureStatusModified` for valid signatures with file hash mismatches\\n   - `SignatureStatusUnsigned` for plugins without MANIFEST.txt\\n\\n## Key Retrieval System\\n\\nPlugin manifest verification requires public keys. The system supports two modes:\\n\\n**Static Keys** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): The default `KeyRetriever` contains a hard-coded Grafana-signed public key with ID `7e4d0c6a708866e7`. The `GetPublicKey()` method returns this key for Grafana-signed plugins.\\n\\n**Dynamic Keys** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): When enabled via configuration, the `KeyRetriever` downloads public keys from the Grafana.com API endpoint `/plugins/ci/keys`. It caches keys in a key store with a 10-day sync interval. The `downloadKeys()` method retrieves and caches `ManifestKeys` records containing keyId and public key content. The `GetPublicKey()` method looks up keys from the cache, falling back to the default key if not found.\\n\\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go` `Service` acts as a selector, delegating to dynamic keys if enabled, otherwise using static keys.\\n\\n## Signature Validation on Load\\n\\nDuring the plugin loading pipeline, signature validation occurs in two stages:\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): The `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` method calls `signatureCalculator.Calculate()` to compute the signature status for each plugin. This populates the plugin's `Signature`, `SignatureType`, and `SignatureOrg` fields.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` and `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): The `Validation.ValidateSignature()` method is called for each bootstrapped plugin. It:\\n\\n1. Returns nil (success) if signature is valid or plugin is core\\n2. For unsigned plugins: calls `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin()` to check the allowlist\\n3. Returns error for invalid or modified signatures\\n4. Handles inherited signatures for nested child plugins\\n\\nThe validation pipeline is orchestrated in `pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/validation.go` through the `Validate()` method, which runs all configured validation steps including `SignatureValidationStep()`.\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement\\n\\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is implemented in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` through the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct. The `CanLoadPlugin()` method enforces the allowlist by:\\n\\n1. Allowing all plugins if signature status is not unsigned (already signed/valid)\\n2. Allowing all unsigned plugins in development mode (when `DevMode` is true)\\n3. Checking the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` list from configuration: if the plugin ID matches an entry in this list, it returns true\\n4. Returning false (rejecting the plugin) otherwise\\n\\nThe configuration is read in `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go` from the INI file key `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` and stored in `pkg/setting/setting.go` as part of the `Cfg` struct's `PluginsAllowUnsigned` field. This configuration is passed to `pkg/plugins/config/config.go` through `PluginManagementCfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned`.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline Integration\\n\\nThe complete signature verification chain is orchestrated in `pkg/plugins/manager/loader/loader.go`. The `Load()` method:\\n\\n1. Discovers plugins\\n2. Bootstraps them (calculating signatures)\\n3. Validates them (checking signatures and enforcing allowlists)\\n4. Initializes them\\n\\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/loader/loader.go` `Loader` wraps this implementation and provides the `Load()` interface for the broader plugin integration system.\\n\\n## Model Definitions\\n\\nSignature-related types are defined in `pkg/plugins/models.go`:\\n- `SignatureStatus`: internal, valid, invalid, modified, unsigned\\n- `SignatureType`: grafana, commercial, community, private, private-glob\\n- `Signature`: struct containing status, type, and signing organization\\n\\nThese types are used throughout the system to track and enforce plugin signature verification.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
